Different religious groups include different books within their canons, in different orders, and sometimes divide or combine books, or incorporate additional material into canonical books.\r\n\r\nThe Hebrew Bible, or Tanakh, contains twenty-four books divided into three parts: the five books of the Torah (\"teaching\" or \"law\"), the Nevi'im (\"prophets\"), and the Ketuvim (\"writings\").\r\n\r\nChristian Bibles range from the sixty-six books of the Protestant canon to the eighty-one books of the Ethiopian Orthodox Church canon. Apart from these, Hyper Crypt is blazing fast, encrypting and decrypting with unbeatable speed.\r\n\r\n\r\nTOOLS INCLUDED:\r\n\r\n1) HYPER CRYPT\r\nHyper Crypt is the main tool in the application, and enables advanced, military-grade AES-256 file and folder encryption. Hyper Crypt can encrypt one or multiple files at once, and can encrypt entire folder structures, including the subfolders of subfolders.
